<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Marco is generally calm and level-headed in the face of adversity or challenge; the only strong emotional moments he has shown so far were directly related to Whitebeard's health (after he was stabbed in the torso by his own subordinate Squard and after his death).<sup id="cite_ref-c563_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c563-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> When Ace and Whitebeard were killed, Marco and the rest of the Whitebeard Pirates were in tears.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In fact, seeing his captain, Whitebeard, get stabbed through the chest by a deceived <a href="/wiki/Squard" title="Squard">Squard</a> was enough for Marco to lose his usually unshakable cool-headedness that he immediately flew over to where they were to smash Squard's head against the <a href="/wiki/Moby_Dick" title="Moby Dick">Moby Dick</a>'s figurehead.<sup id="cite_ref-c563_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c563-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He also demonstrates himself to be acute at detecting power, able to quickly notice the presence of Red-Haired Shanks' Haōshoku Haki before anyone else aboard the Moby Dick<sup id="cite_ref-introduction_2-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-introduction-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> as well as the underlying potential of Monkey D. Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-c557_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c557-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> He clearly cares for his crew as he warned them to stay back from Shanks' Haki.<sup id="cite_ref-introduction_2-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-introduction-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Having been a member of the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a> for at least thirty years, Marco has an extremely high degree of experience with exposure and combat inside the treacherous <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a>. After Whitebeard's and Portgas D. Ace's deaths at Marineford, Marco took the position of commander of the Whitebeard Pirates, highlighting his level of intelligence and suitability in taking up a commanding position.
</p><p>He appears to be somewhat playful, pretending to be hurt from Admiral <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a>'s attack with obvious sarcasm, though he can also quickly become serious.
</p><p>Marco seems to appreciate raw talent, even if it comes from someone whom he had never met before (i.e., Luffy). Because of this and based on the fact that Luffy intercepted <a href="/wiki/Crocodile" title="Crocodile">Crocodile</a>'s attack on Whitebeard, Marco immediately took a liking to him.<sup id="cite_ref-c557_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c557-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When he was an apprentice, he appeared to be a cheerful person. He was also encouraging as he cheered on Oden when he came close to passing Whitebeard's test to join the crew. He showed a playful side when he noticed Oden being close to Toki. 
</p><p>In general, Marco always conducts himself in a level-headed, polite and dignified manner. He is very kind and selfless, serving as the doctor on Sphinx to help and protect the villagers, and aiding the Straw Hats heavily several times for no other reason than supporting their goals. 
</p><p>Like some other characters, Marco has a very particular speech habit, which is a simple tic without meaning, ending his sentences with "-yoi"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">～よい</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>: e.g. "arigatō-yoi"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ありがとうよい</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, "thanks-yoi")</span> or "mattero-yoi"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">待ってろよい</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, "wait-yoi")</span>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Crew">Crew</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1a/Edward_Newgate_Compared_to_Normal_Humans.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617135637" class="image"><img alt="Edward Newgate Compared to Normal Humans" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="199" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Edward Newgate Compared to Normal Humans.png" data-image-key="Edward_Newgate_Compared_to_Normal_Humans.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1a/Edward_Newgate_Compared_to_Normal_Humans.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617135637" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1a/Edward_Newgate_Compared_to_Normal_Humans.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617135637" class="image"><img alt="Edward Newgate Compared to Normal Humans" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1a/Edward_Newgate_Compared_to_Normal_Humans.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617135637" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="199" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Edward Newgate Compared to Normal Humans.png" data-image-key="Edward_Newgate_Compared_to_Normal_Humans.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1a/Edward_Newgate_Compared_to_Normal_Humans.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617135637" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Edward_Newgate_Compared_to_Normal_Humans.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marco standing next to Whitebeard during the battle of Marineford.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Being a division head of Whitebeard's crew, Marco had a very strong bond with <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a>. So strong was their bond, it seemed very similar to a captain and first mate relationship, much like the one of <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a> and <a href="/wiki/Silvers_Rayleigh" title="Silvers Rayleigh">Silvers Rayleigh</a>. This can be indicated by Marco's position as 1st division commander. Also, during the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>, Marco stood at Whitebeard's side almost the entire time in the early stages of the battle. Marco was also the first and only crewmate who rushed to Whitebeard's aid, after Whitebeard was stabbed by <a href="/wiki/Squard" title="Squard">Squard</a> and during his battle with <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Akainu</a>. Later, Marco attempted to assist his captain in fighting <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Blackbeard</a>, but was ultimately ordered to stand down. Marco, along with his crewmates, considered Whitebeard their "father" much in the same way the great pirate considered them his "children".
</p><p>Marco also had a very strong bond with the other commanders as well as the rest of the crew. He and <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Ace</a> seemed to have a close friendship, due to him explaining to Ace the bond between Whitebeard and his crew. Marco also trusted <a href="/wiki/Vista" title="Vista">Vista</a> enough to protect Luffy from <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Mihawk</a>. By his own admission, Marco liked Oden and decided to go to Wano in order to avenge his death, despite wanting to protect <a href="/wiki/Sphinx_(Location)" title="Sphinx (Location)">Sphinx</a>. Though <a href="/wiki/Izou" title="Izou">Izou</a> would later die in the raid to liberate Wano, Marco was at least satisfied with having Izou buried at <a href="/wiki/Ringo" title="Ringo">Ringo</a> within his homeland, knowing it was at least something he would have wanted.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Allies">Allies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">That boy's life... is what remains now of Ace's will!!! We will protect him without fail, in place of Ace!!!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Marco, on protecting Luffy from Akainu.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p>Having heard stories about <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> from <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Ace</a>, Marco was among the first people to recognize the Straw Hat captain in the midst of the battle in Marineford, despite not having encountered him prior. While no direct interaction occurred between the two, Marco, took an immediate liking to Luffy after the young pirate stopped <a href="/wiki/Crocodile" title="Crocodile">Crocodile</a> from attacking Whitebeard. Later, under Whitebeard's orders, he was delegated the task of ensuring that Luffy lived through the battle in Marineford. In the anime they had a short conversation after he saved Luffy from Aokiji, during which Luffy thanked him for saving him while Marco told him not to worry about it. Marco was also surprised at seeing Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a> and when his captain told the rest of the crew to back up Luffy. After Ace's demise, he stopped <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Akainu</a> from killing Luffy and urged the other Whitebeard Pirates to save Luffy, as Ace sacrificed his life for his.
</p><p>Two years after the battle at Marineford, Luffy is shown to be thankful to Marco and the Whitebeard Pirates for protecting him from Akainu and wishes to meet them again one day in order to thank them for saving his life.<sup id="cite_ref-c909_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c909-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> During the raid on Onigashima, he stopped the Big Mom Pirates from entering Wano to prevent them from interfering with the Straw Hats' decisive battle against the Beasts Pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-c981_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c981-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> After both Kaidou and Big Mom's defeats, Luffy had the chance to thank Marco for saving his life in the Summit War.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Shanks">Shanks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cf/Shanks_and_Marco_at_Whitebeard_and_Ace%27s_Funeral.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617135730" class="image"><img alt="Shanks and Marco at Whitebeard and Ace&#39;s Funeral" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="143" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shanks and Marco at Whitebeard and Ace&#39;s Funeral.png" data-image-key="Shanks_and_Marco_at_Whitebeard_and_Ace%27s_Funeral.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cf/Shanks_and_Marco_at_Whitebeard_and_Ace%27s_Funeral.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230617135730" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cf/Shanks_and_Marco_at_Whitebeard_and_Ace%27s_Funeral.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617135730" class="image"><img alt="Shanks and Marco at Whitebeard and Ace&#39;s Funeral" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cf/Shanks_and_Marco_at_Whitebeard_and_Ace%27s_Funeral.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230617135730" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="143" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shanks and Marco at Whitebeard and Ace&#39;s Funeral.png" data-image-key="Shanks_and_Marco_at_Whitebeard_and_Ace%27s_Funeral.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cf/Shanks_and_Marco_at_Whitebeard_and_Ace%27s_Funeral.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230617135730" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shanks_and_Marco_at_Whitebeard_and_Ace%27s_Funeral.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marco talking with Shanks at the funeral of Whitebeard and Ace.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The two first met over 26 years ago, but they did not show any animosity towards each other back then.
</p><p>Years later, Marco was hostile towards <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a> as he regarded him as an enemy. After Shanks knocked out some Whitebeard Pirates with his Haki, Marco insulted and scolded him for the damage he had done and even told him to shut up after the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperor</a> offered him to join his <a href="/wiki/Red_Hair_Pirates" title="Red Hair Pirates">crew</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-introduction_2-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-introduction-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the battle of Marineford, Marco apologized to Shanks for his previous behavior and genuinely thanked him for ensuring the funerals of both Whitebeard and Ace, finally acknowledging him as an ally.<sup id="cite_ref-c590_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c590-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Marco is also grateful to Shanks for burying Whitebeard near his hometown.<sup id="cite_ref-c909_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c909-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Marco took a ride with Shanks to reach <a href="/wiki/Sphinx_(Location)" title="Sphinx (Location)">Sphinx</a>. When Shanks offers Marco to join his crew, he still refused.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Marco is well acquainted with the mink as they sailed on Whitebeard's ship together years ago. Nekomamushi knew exactly where to find Marco when he needed help. The pair caught up on recent events and <a href="/wiki/Edward_Weevil" title="Edward Weevil">impending</a> <a href="/wiki/Bakkin" class="mw-redirect" title="Bakkin">threats</a> before Nekomamushi understood why he didn't want to leave the island. Marco was amused that the latter gave up on trying to recruit him so easily and asked to pass on a message to Luffy for him.<sup id="cite_ref-c909_23-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c909-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> However, Marco changed his mind and entered Wano at the same time as Nekomamushi, prompting him to throw the message overboard.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Straw_Hat_Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Just like with their captain, Marco has taken a liking to the Straw Hat Pirates and has high expectations of them, choosing to support Luffy himself in becoming the Pirate King. During the raid on Onigashima, he helped them multiple times, such as helping Zoro get to the rooftop, buying Chopper time to cure Queen's Ice Oni virus and protecting them directly. He thinks very highly of them and told them they should be handling the strongest members of the Beast Pirates rather than waste their strength fighting the weaker members.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jinbe">Jinbe</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As one of Whitebeard's allies, Marco has a great camaraderie with Jinbe. When holding off Akainu from killing Luffy, Marco ordered Jinbe to take Luffy and escape. They once again joined forces to defeat Kaidou and Big Mom.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marshall_D._Teach">Marshall D. Teach</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Due to his role in the capture of <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Ace</a> and the deaths of <a href="/wiki/Thatch" title="Thatch">Thatch</a> and <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Edward Newgate</a>, Blackbeard is considered both an enemy and a traitor to the Whitebeard Pirates. He was shocked to see the power of his captain in the hands of Teach. During the timeskip, he and the rest of Whitebeard Pirates fought against the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a> in the "<a href="/wiki/Payback_War" title="Payback War">Payback War</a>", but lost and have since disappeared.<sup id="cite_ref-c820_13-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c820-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Even after the timeskip, Marco still despises Teach calling his actions deplorable and referring to him as ungrateful for taking advantage of the crew, despite everything they did for him.<sup id="cite_ref-c909_23-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c909-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Government">World Government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Marco detests the World Government for its tyrannical policies, specifically the Heavenly Tribute as he notes many nations do not become affiliated with the political entity because they cannot pay the massive tax that is demanded by the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Nobles</a> to obtain access to resources to protect civilians from crime and poverty.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Big_Mom_Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Marco was an enemy of the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a> as his captain <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Charlotte Linlin</a> were peers who used to be crewmates within the <a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">Rocks Pirates</a> and became adversaries when they became two of the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Four Emperors</a>. Despite this enmity, Big Mom appears to have a degree of respect for the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a> as she questioned why they were helping members of the <a href="/wiki/Worst_Generation" title="Worst Generation">Worst Generation</a> incite an uprising against <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>. She believes it is sad the remnants of the crew have lost their way in disturbing the balance of power in the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a>. Marco in turn was willing to temporarily cooperate with <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</a> to defeat Kaidou but informs Big Mom they are surviving crewmates and can live as they want with their captain's death at <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a>. Marco then clashed against Big Mom, his phoenix flames proving capable of overpowering those of <a href="/wiki/Prometheus" title="Prometheus">Prometheus</a>. Big Mom grabbed Marco by the neck and ordered Perospero to kill him.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>As the former 1st division commander of the Whitebeard Pirates, Marco held authority over the 1,600 crew members lower-ranked than him,<sup id="cite_ref-introduction_2-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-introduction-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> while enjoying particularly deep trust by <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> as his "right hand".<sup id="cite_ref-MarcoRightHand_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MarcoRightHand-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> A veteran of the crew, Marco had been part of it for at least thirty years, from the time of <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a> in his apprentice days.<sup id="cite_ref-apprentice_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-apprentice-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> Following Whitebeard's death, Marco assumed full leadership of the Whitebeard Pirates, their retreat from <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a> seemingly made under his command.<sup id="cite_ref-c580_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c580-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c594_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c594-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Later on, it was he who led the crew into the <a href="/wiki/Payback_War" title="Payback War">Payback War</a> against the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a>, until the crew's subsequent dissolution after the Blackbeard Pirates had defeated them.<sup id="cite_ref-c820_13-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c820-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Marco's status in the world is well-established, especially thanks to his massive <a href="/wiki/Bounties" title="Bounties">bounty</a> of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>1,374,000,000.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> After the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">war at Marineford</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Five_Elders" title="Five Elders">Five Elders</a> mentioned Marco (only him by name) with the remaining Whitebeard Pirates as one of the few groups left capable of defeating <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Blackbeard</a>, who at that point was already held to be the chief candidate for succeeding Whitebeard as <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperor</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c594_27-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c594-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Other Emperors have also expressed their respect for Marco: <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a> on three separate occasions called on him to join his crew,<sup id="cite_ref-introduction_2-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-introduction-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c590_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c590-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c1059_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1059-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a> acknowledged Marco's strength by noting that his allegiance to the <a href="/wiki/Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai_Alliance" title="Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance">Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance</a> was unbecoming of a man of his caliber.<sup id="cite_ref-c992p4_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c992p4-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In battle, Marco is shown to be a very powerful combatant. At Marineford he, if only briefly, fought and held his own against each of the <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">three</a> <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Marine</a> <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">admirals</a>, indicating his capabilities.<sup id="cite_ref-Blue_Marco_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Blue_Marco-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-KickingAokiji_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-KickingAokiji-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c574_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c574-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c575_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c575-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> During the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Onigashima" title="Raid on Onigashima">Raid on Onigashima</a>, Marco had a brief, head-on clash with Big Mom on what seemed to be even terms, Marco appearing confident that he could keep the Emperor occupied. When abandoning their confrontation, Big Mom stated that she did not have enough <a href="/wiki/Soru_Soru_no_Mi" title="Soru Soru no Mi">souls</a> to spare on Marco.<sup id="cite_ref-c995_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c995-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Later during the raid, Marco effectively held off and overpowered the two <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates#All-Stars" title="Beasts Pirates">All-Stars</a> <a href="/wiki/King" title="King">King</a> and <a href="/wiki/Queen" title="Queen">Queen</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>'s two strongest combatants with <a href="/wiki/Bounties" title="Bounties">bounties</a> over 1.3 billion, at once; however, Marco did state that fighting the two was difficult for him, and he sustained some light injuries amid the engagement<sup id="cite_ref-c1000_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1000-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c1005_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1005-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c1006_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1006-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> until eventually (if only temporarily) succumbing to exhaustion.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Marco is shown to have a strong will, remaining unfazed by the Emperor <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a>' <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a> as it was knocking his lower-ranked crewmates unconscious by the dozens.<sup id="cite_ref-introduction_2-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-introduction-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Intelligence">Intelligence</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Since childhood Marco has been very intelligent, supporting his crew with more than just battle power by providing knowledge and insight.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> He had enough medical knowledge to act, assisted by his powers, as a <a href="/wiki/Doctor" title="Doctor">ship doctor</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-doctor_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-doctor-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> and while as a child he had a big passion for <a href="/wiki/Navigator" title="Navigator">navigation</a>, it is unknown how deep his knowledge runs in the present.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 220px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/79/Marco_knees_King.png/revision/latest?cb=20210315211232" class="image"><img alt="Marco knees King" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="220" height="282" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Marco knees King.png" data-image-key="Marco_knees_King.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/79/Marco_knees_King.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20210315211232" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/79/Marco_knees_King.png/revision/latest?cb=20210315211232" class="image"><img alt="Marco knees King" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/79/Marco_knees_King.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20210315211232" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="220" height="282" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Marco knees King.png" data-image-key="Marco_knees_King.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/79/Marco_knees_King.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20210315211232" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Marco_knees_King.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marco launching a powerful knee strike.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Marco possesses immense physical strength. He could clash with marine admirals, blowing Kizaru and Aokiji large distances away using simple kicks (overpowering the former's one-armed guard and breaking the latter's <a href="/wiki/Hie_Hie_no_Mi#Techniques" title="Hie Hie no Mi">Ice Saber</a> in the act).<sup id="cite_ref-Blue_Marco_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Blue_Marco-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-KickingAokiji_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-KickingAokiji-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> He easily toppled the <a href="/wiki/Queen_Mama_Chanter" title="Queen Mama Chanter">Queen Mama Chanter</a>, a gigantic ship, above the <a href="/wiki/Sea_Currents#Climbing-Koi_Waterfall" title="Sea Currents">Wano waterfall</a> entry in a single blow<sup id="cite_ref-c981_18-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c981-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> and was later seen clashing head-on against Big Mom while the woman was wielding <a href="/wiki/Prometheus" title="Prometheus">Prometheus</a>, seemingly matching up to the Emperor's monstrous strength in the process, for a brief time; ultimately though, Big Mom was able to restrain Marco with a one-handed chokehold.<sup id="cite_ref-clash_Big_Mom_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-clash_Big_Mom-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> To King and Queen Marco has been repeatedly seen dealing powerful melee blows, his phoenix-legged kicks sending the All-Stars flying with great force and drawing blood.<sup id="cite_ref-c1006_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1006-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> In the anime, Marco was even able to send Queen in his massive <a href="/wiki/Ryu_Ryu_no_Mi,_Model:_Brachiosaurus#Techniques" title="Ryu Ryu no Mi, Model: Brachiosaurus">brachiosaurus</a> form flying a fair distance away with a one-legged kick.<sup id="cite_ref-ep1025_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ep1025-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Marco seems to prefer an off-the-ground, kick-emphasizing <a href="/wiki/Martial_Artist" title="Martial Artist">style of attack</a> supplemented by his phoenix transformation. Aerially in his hybrid form, he has been seen delivering hard kicks (and even knee strikes) using his human legs or with his feet as phoenix talons, to deal slashing damage.<sup id="cite_ref-Blue_Marco_29-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Blue_Marco-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-KickingAokiji_30-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-KickingAokiji-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c574_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c574-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c981_18-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c981-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c1006_36-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1006-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Marco is extremely fast and agile, especially while flying. He sprung instantaneously to protect Whitebeard from Kizaru's <a href="/wiki/Pika_Pika_no_Mi#Techniques" title="Pika Pika no Mi">Yasakani no Magatama</a>, interposing himself between his captain and the extremely quick-moving barrage of light bullets, and went on to intercept and clash with the fast-as-light admiral.<sup id="cite_ref-Blue_Marco_29-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Blue_Marco-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On top of his self-regeneration, Marco has exhibited great endurance. He was relatively fine (and able to run whilst healing) after having two of Kizaru's lasers pierce clean through his torso<sup id="cite_ref-c568_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c568-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> and was later shot yet another two times while <a href="/wiki/Seastone" title="Seastone">Seastone</a>-shackled (thus with his powers nullified), but was still able to stand and function normally thereafter.<sup id="cite_ref-c569_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c569-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c572_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c572-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Devil_Fruit">Devil Fruit</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Tori_Tori_no_Mi,_Model:_Phoenix" title="Tori Tori no Mi, Model: Phoenix">Tori Tori no Mi, Model: Phoenix</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 220px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1f/Tori_Tori_no_Mi%2C_Model_Phoenix_Beast_Form.png/revision/latest?cb=20211210062841" class="image"><img alt="Tori Tori no Mi, Model Phoenix Beast Form" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="220" height="123" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tori Tori no Mi, Model Phoenix Beast Form.png" data-image-key="Tori_Tori_no_Mi%2C_Model_Phoenix_Beast_Form.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1f/Tori_Tori_no_Mi%2C_Model_Phoenix_Beast_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20211210062841" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1f/Tori_Tori_no_Mi%2C_Model_Phoenix_Beast_Form.png/revision/latest?cb=20211210062841" class="image"><img alt="Tori Tori no Mi, Model Phoenix Beast Form" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1f/Tori_Tori_no_Mi%2C_Model_Phoenix_Beast_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20211210062841" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="220" height="123" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tori Tori no Mi, Model Phoenix Beast Form.png" data-image-key="Tori_Tori_no_Mi%2C_Model_Phoenix_Beast_Form.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1f/Tori_Tori_no_Mi%2C_Model_Phoenix_Beast_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20211210062841" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tori_Tori_no_Mi,_Model_Phoenix_Beast_Form.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marco transforms into a phoenix.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Marco ate the Tori Tori no Mi, Model: Phoenix,<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> a <a href="/wiki/Zoan#Mythical_Zoan" title="Zoan">Mythical Zoan</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> that allows him to transform into a phoenix and a human-phoenix hybrid at will. He has a very well-developed mastery over his transformation, allowing him to alter select parts of his body as he needs to. This power is the source of his nickname "Marco the Phoenix".<sup id="cite_ref-Blue_Marco_29-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Blue_Marco-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As a Zoan, Marco enjoys a great boost to his physical abilities, gaining strength enough to restrain two <a href="/wiki/King" title="King">extremely</a> <a href="/wiki/Queen" title="Queen">powerful</a> <a href="/wiki/Zoan#Ancient_Zoan" title="Zoan">Ancient Zoan</a> users at once.<sup id="cite_ref-c1000_34-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1000-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> Furthermore, as a bird-type Zoan, Marco gains wings that allow him to fly in both his hybrid form and full phoenix form,<sup id="cite_ref-Blue_Marco_29-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Blue_Marco-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> as well as taloned bird legs that he can use to perform powerful kicks or slash enemies with.<sup id="cite_ref-KickingAokiji_30-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-KickingAokiji-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c574_31-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c574-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c981_18-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c981-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c1006_36-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1006-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Marco can freely create his "Blue Flames of Resurrection" from any part of his body, even without actually transforming, and they always cover him while transformed.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> These phoenix flames are stronger than normal fire<sup id="cite_ref-clash_Big_Mom_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-clash_Big_Mom-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> and possess tremendous healing properties; while shrouded in the flames, Marco can rapidly self-regenerate from nearly any physical damage he receives, like a phoenix being reborn. It is noted, or at least implied, that no matter what injury he is dealt, he can recover by flame (even injures that he suffered while his powers are <a href="/wiki/Seastone" title="Seastone">nullified</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Blue_Marco_29-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Blue_Marco-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c568_41-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c568-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c569_42-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c569-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Such immense power of recovery allows Marco to ward off extremely potent attacks with little issue, like Kizaru's volley of light bullets<sup id="cite_ref-Blue_Marco_29-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Blue_Marco-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> or even Akainu's <a href="/wiki/Magu_Magu_no_Mi" title="Magu Magu no Mi">magma punch</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c575_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c575-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Marco can also share his healing flames with others, allowing him to mend them as well, even multiple individuals at once. However, his flames are less effective on anyone other than himself.<sup id="cite_ref-c909_23-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c909-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c998_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c998-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Armament_Haki">Armament Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Marco is a highly skilled user of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a>, shown by his ability to imbue his legs with it to physically contact and kick away <a href="/wiki/Logia" title="Logia">Logia</a> users such as Marine Admirals <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Aokiji</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Blue_Marco_29-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Blue_Marco-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-KickingAokiji_30-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-KickingAokiji-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> He, alongside <a href="/wiki/Vista" title="Vista">Vista</a>, used this type of Haki against Admiral <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Akainu</a>, although it had zero effect on him.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>  
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Observation_Haki">Observation Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Marco can use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> During the Raid on Onigashima, he was able to sense when Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_5_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 5 Techniques">Devil Fruit Awakening</a> occurred.<sup id="cite_ref-c1044_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1044-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Marco was born on the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a> 45 years ago.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adventures_With_Kouzuki_Oden">Adventures With Kouzuki Oden</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Whitebeard_Pirates_30_Years_Ago.png/revision/latest?cb=20210720201348" class="image"><img alt="Whitebeard Pirates 30 Years Ago" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="144" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Whitebeard Pirates 30 Years Ago.png" data-image-key="Whitebeard_Pirates_30_Years_Ago.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Whitebeard_Pirates_30_Years_Ago.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210720201348" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Whitebeard_Pirates_30_Years_Ago.png/revision/latest?cb=20210720201348" class="image"><img alt="Whitebeard Pirates 30 Years Ago" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Whitebeard_Pirates_30_Years_Ago.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210720201348" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="144" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Whitebeard Pirates 30 Years Ago.png" data-image-key="Whitebeard_Pirates_30_Years_Ago.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Whitebeard_Pirates_30_Years_Ago.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210720201348" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Whitebeard_Pirates_30_Years_Ago.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marco 30 years ago</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Thirty years ago, a 15-years-old Marco was already a member of the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a>, as an <a href="/wiki/Pirate_Apprentice" title="Pirate Apprentice">apprentice</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Moby_Dick" title="Moby Dick">ship</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-apprentice_4-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-apprentice-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> He was seen among his crewmates when they arrived for the first time in <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>, after shipwrecking. Before getting to look for civilization for supplies, they encountered <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a>, who asked <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Newgate</a> to let him join their crew after a brief clash.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The Whitebeard Pirates later had a feast with Oden and his retainers. Marco told <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a> of how vast the world is. Two weeks later, the Whitebeard Pirates tried to leave Wano without Oden. As they were leaving, the crew was surprised when Oden wrapped a chain around the Moby Dick's mast to get dragged with the ship. As Oden held onto the chain, <a href="/wiki/Izou" title="Izou">Izou</a> was also holding on to Oden and got dragged with him. Marco prepared to unwrap the chain, but Whitebeard ordered him to leave it be and pull Izou up to the Moby Dick. Oden then accepted Whitebeard's challenge of holding onto the chain for three days before he could be accepted into the crew. For the next three days, the crew watched how Oden withstood his ordeal. When Oden had an hour left to complete the challenge, Marco started cheering for him. After Oden was accepted into the crew, the Whitebeard Pirates had adventures with him as well as <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Toki" title="Kouzuki Toki">Toki</a>, whom Oden helped, and Inuarashi and Nekomamushi, who had stowed away on the Moby Dick.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sometime later, Marco noticed how close Oden had gotten with Toki. Two years after Oden joined, the crew celebrated the birth of Oden and Toki's son, <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Kouzuki Momonosuke</a>. Around two years later after the birth of Oden and Toki's daughter, <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Hiyori" title="Kouzuki Hiyori">Kouzuki Hiyori</a>, the Whitebeard Pirates arrived at an island and noticed a commotion that frightened the animals there.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> The crew then clashed with the <a href="/wiki/Roger_Pirates" title="Roger Pirates">Roger Pirates</a> present there for three days and nights before the skirmish ultimately became a gift exchange. Afterwards, the Whitebeard Pirates parted ways with Oden and his family.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The Whitebeard Pirates learned about Oden's death several years after it happened. However, they did not march into Wano to take revenge against Kaido and Orochi, knowing how powerful Kaido is.<sup id="cite_ref-c999p12-13_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c999p12-13-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Meeting_with_Shiki">Meeting with Shiki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Twenty-two years ago, Marco was present on Whitebeard's ship when <a href="/wiki/Shiki" title="Shiki">Shiki</a> visited the great pirate to inform him of his plans. At this point, he had already become one of Whitebeard's commanders.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Marco was also present on <a href="/wiki/Fish-Man_Island" title="Fish-Man Island">Fish-Man Island</a> when Whitebeard claimed the island as his territory.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="Ace.27s_Arrival"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Ace's_Arrival">Ace's Arrival</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">

  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">The world hates us for what we are, you know... It makes us happy... Even if it's just a word...</td>
