<p><br />
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/67/Marco_Talks_to_Ace.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617140035" class="image"><img alt="Marco Talks to Ace" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="127" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Marco Talks to Ace.png" data-image-key="Marco_Talks_to_Ace.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/67/Marco_Talks_to_Ace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617140035" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/67/Marco_Talks_to_Ace.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617140035" class="image"><img alt="Marco Talks to Ace" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/67/Marco_Talks_to_Ace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617140035" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="127" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Marco Talks to Ace.png" data-image-key="Marco_Talks_to_Ace.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/67/Marco_Talks_to_Ace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617140035" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Marco_Talks_to_Ace.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marco tells Ace to make a decision.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the first few days that <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Portgas D. Ace</a> came to spend on Whitebeard's ship, Marco tried to befriend him. Marco explained to Ace the kind of fatherly relationship Whitebeard had with his <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">crew members</a>. In fact, it was Marco who told Ace to leave the ship and start from scratch again or bear Whitebeard's mark as one of his sons.<sup id="cite_ref-c552_17-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c552-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At some point, Ace talked with Whitebeard about going to war with Kaidou to liberate Wano Country, but Whitebeard never agreed to this request. Marco stated that he would join Ace if Whitebeard gave his approval.<sup id="cite_ref-c999p12-13_52-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c999p12-13-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> At another point three and a half years before the current storyline, Ace defeated a former <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the sea</a>, causing said warlord to be removed from his position. Six months later, Marco alongside Ace, Whitebeard, Teach, and Jinbe learned that a <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">replacement</a> for the warlord was decided.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="Thatch.27s_Murder"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Thatch's_Murder">Thatch's Murder</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After the murder of <a href="/wiki/Thatch" title="Thatch">Thatch</a> at the hands of <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Marshall D. Teach</a>, Ace decided to search for Blackbeard and make him pay for what he did. However, Whitebeard, who was feeling uneasy, told Ace not to go, something that Ace did not want to hear. Marco was one of the crew members who protested to Ace leaving the ship and going after Teach, but this was in vain.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sky_Island_Saga">Sky Island Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jaya_Arc">Jaya Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Marco was aboard Whitebeard's ship when <a href="/wiki/Rockstar" title="Rockstar">Rockstar</a> delivered a letter from <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a>. Rockstar boasted about his own notoriety, but Marco claimed to have never heard of him.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Water_7_Saga">Water 7 Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-Enies_Lobby_Arc">Post-Enies Lobby Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>When Shanks came to visit Whitebeard personally, Marco and <a href="/wiki/Jozu" title="Jozu">Jozu</a> warned the younger and weaker crew members to stay back due to Shanks's <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">overwhelming presence</a>. He also told the members still standing afterward not to worry about their fallen comrades as they were just unconscious. Marco scolded Shanks for what he did to his subordinates, and Shanks recognized him as the 1st division commander and asked him if he would like to join the <a href="/wiki/Red_Hair_Pirates" title="Red Hair Pirates">Red Hair Pirates</a>, which Marco refused.<sup id="cite_ref-introduction_2-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-introduction-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Summit_War_Saga">Summit War Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marineford_Arc">Marineford Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9b/Borsalino_vs._Marco.png/revision/latest?cb=20230519052206" class="image"><img alt="Borsalino vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Borsalino vs. Marco.png" data-image-key="Borsalino_vs._Marco.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9b/Borsalino_vs._Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230519052206" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9b/Borsalino_vs._Marco.png/revision/latest?cb=20230519052206" class="image"><img alt="Borsalino vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9b/Borsalino_vs._Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230519052206" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Borsalino vs. Marco.png" data-image-key="Borsalino_vs._Marco.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9b/Borsalino_vs._Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230519052206" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Borsalino_vs._Marco.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marco battles Kizaru.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Marco showed up at <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a> with the rest of the Whitebeard Pirates and their subordinate crews from the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a>. He stated that, including him, all of the Whitebeard Pirates were ready to battle anyone who had dared to lay a single finger on Ace. Later, when <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a> tried to attack Whitebeard with an <a href="/wiki/Pika_Pika_no_Mi" title="Pika Pika no Mi">array of laser beams</a>, Marco nullified the attack with his powerful <a href="/wiki/Tori_Tori_no_Mi,_Model:_Phoenix" title="Tori Tori no Mi, Model: Phoenix">Devil Fruit transformation</a>. He then proceeded to assault Kizaru, successfully kicking him a great distance to the ground, though the <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">admiral</a> did not appear seriously injured by the act.<sup id="cite_ref-Blue_Marco_29-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Blue_Marco-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sometime thereafter, Marco saw <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> and his <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a> team falling from the sky and came to the realization that Ace's brother, whom Ace had always talked about, had arrived. When he witnessed Luffy stopping <a href="/wiki/Crocodile" title="Crocodile">Crocodile</a>'s attempt to kill Whitebeard on the grounds of Whitebeard being important to Ace, Marco concluded that, "Ace's little brother is not too shabby after all".<sup id="cite_ref-c557_21-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c557-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Just after Luffy had dashed off after informing Whitebeard that Ace would be executed ahead of schedule, Marco returned to the <a href="/wiki/Moby_Dick" title="Moby Dick">Moby Dick</a> to report the same news. Whitebeard, after seeing some of Luffy's resolve to save Ace, told Marco that he would not forgive him if he were to let Luffy die, to which Marco (who appeared to have developed a similar opinion and liking towards Luffy) smiled and replied, "Roger."
</p><p>Later, after Whitebeard manipulated <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy</a> into joining his cause temporarily, Marco remarked at how simple-minded Buggy was.<sup id="cite_ref-c558_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c558-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> When he witnessed Luffy being attacked by <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</a>, he called out to 5th division commander <a href="/wiki/Vista" title="Vista">Vista</a> to go and help him out.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> Afterwards, Marco found it odd when <a href="/wiki/Squard" title="Squard">Squard</a> appeared next to Whitebeard and was shocked when Whitebeard was stabbed by him.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> He was the first one to reach the Moby Dick and to incapacitate Squard, but he was repelled by Squard's sword when Squard told Marco it was also his fault that he had been forced to attack Whitebeard.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Marco_vs._Kuzan.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617140237" class="image"><img alt="Marco vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Marco vs. Kuzan.png" data-image-key="Marco_vs._Kuzan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Marco_vs._Kuzan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230617140237" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Marco_vs._Kuzan.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617140237" class="image"><img alt="Marco vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Marco_vs._Kuzan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230617140237" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Marco vs. Kuzan.png" data-image-key="Marco_vs._Kuzan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Marco_vs._Kuzan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230617140237" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Marco_vs._Kuzan.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marco kicks Aokiji to save Luffy.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Crocodile yelled at Whitebeard for being weak, Marco commented on how Whitebeard's health was getting worse, since Whitebeard should have been able to stop any attack aimed at him, even if he was caught off-guard.<sup id="cite_ref-c563_19-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c563-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> After the whole ordeal was sorted out, he saw Squard crying and deeply regretting his actions, and suggested to him that he should redeem himself.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> Thereafter, Marco's expression was solemn when he witnessed the Moby Dick being destroyed by <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Akainu</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Magu_Magu_no_Mi" title="Magu Magu no Mi">meteoric magma attack</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Later, as Ace was about to be executed, Marco was prepared to swoop in and save him, but noted that he was not needed after <a href="/wiki/Crocodile" title="Crocodile">Crocodile</a> saved Ace first. After Luffy was heavily injured by the admirals and was about to be finished off by <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Aokiji</a>, Marco arrived and kicked Aokiji away a great distance.<sup id="cite_ref-KickingAokiji_30-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-KickingAokiji-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Garp_Punches_Marco.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617140406" class="image"><img alt="Garp Punches Marco" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp Punches Marco.png" data-image-key="Garp_Punches_Marco.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Garp_Punches_Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230617140406" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Garp_Punches_Marco.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617140406" class="image"><img alt="Garp Punches Marco" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Garp_Punches_Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230617140406" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp Punches Marco.png" data-image-key="Garp_Punches_Marco.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a4/Garp_Punches_Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230617140406" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_Punches_Marco.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp sends Marco crashing down.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Eventually, with (seemingly) only two <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> watching over Ace, Marco flew towards the execution platform telling Ace that he would soon save him. As he got closer, however, <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Monkey D. Garp</a> intercepted him with a punch that sent him crashing to the ground. Marco, now in human form, looked up, frustrated and with a bruise on the left side of his chin.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c2/Borsalino_Attacks_Marco.png/revision/latest?cb=20230524011417" class="image"><img alt="Borsalino Attacks Marco" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="117" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Borsalino Attacks Marco.png" data-image-key="Borsalino_Attacks_Marco.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c2/Borsalino_Attacks_Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230524011417" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c2/Borsalino_Attacks_Marco.png/revision/latest?cb=20230524011417" class="image"><img alt="Borsalino Attacks Marco" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c2/Borsalino_Attacks_Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230524011417" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="117" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Borsalino Attacks Marco.png" data-image-key="Borsalino_Attacks_Marco.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c2/Borsalino_Attacks_Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230524011417" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Borsalino_Attacks_Marco.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kizaru pierces a distracted Marco.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the midst of battling Akainu suddenly seized Whitebeard's chest and Marco, in horror, realized what was happening just as Whitebeard coughed up a massive amount of blood. Marco thought to himself that this was what he was most afraid might happen and rushed towards his captain. However, he did not get very far before Kizaru shot him from behind with two simultaneous lasers, which clearly caused Marco pain, as he was in his human form.<sup id="cite_ref-c568_41-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c568-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Enduring the pain, Marco activated his regenerative powers and continued to run towards Whitebeard, only to have <a href="/wiki/Onigumo" title="Onigumo">Onigumo</a> seize him and place <a href="/wiki/Seastone" title="Seastone">Seastone</a> handcuffs on his right arm. Kizaru then took the opportunity to shoot Marco with yet two more laser bursts. Badly injured and unable to regenerate, Marco fell.<sup id="cite_ref-c569_42-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c569-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later on, after Luffy unconsciously used his <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>, the bloodied Marco showed surprise. By the time Squard entered the battlefield with the paddle boat <a href="/wiki/Little_Oars_Jr." title="Little Oars Jr.">Little Oars Jr.</a> brought into the plaza, stating that Whitebeard and his subordinate crews should grab Ace and leave the enemy to him, Marco was back on his feet. He commented angrily on Squard's foolish way of redeeming himself and quickly ordered a nearby crewmate to remove his cuffs.<sup id="cite_ref-c572_43-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c572-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Whitebeard declared that he would part ways with his sons and stay behind, Marco hesitated, reluctant, as a nearby crewmate urged him to go. Soon after, Marco was shocked by the sight of Ace taking Akainu's molten rock punch through the chest.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> Then when Akainu tried to strike Ace a second time and finish him off, he was stopped by Jinbe; Marco saw this and, desperate now, ordered <a href="/wiki/Galdino" title="Galdino">Galdino</a>, who was dragged over to him, to remove his handcuffs immediately.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/01/Akainu_Attacked_With_Haki.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617141116" class="image"><img alt="Akainu Attacked With Haki" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Akainu Attacked With Haki.png" data-image-key="Akainu_Attacked_With_Haki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/01/Akainu_Attacked_With_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617141116" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/01/Akainu_Attacked_With_Haki.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617141116" class="image"><img alt="Akainu Attacked With Haki" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/01/Akainu_Attacked_With_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617141116" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Akainu Attacked With Haki.png" data-image-key="Akainu_Attacked_With_Haki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/01/Akainu_Attacked_With_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617141116" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Akainu_Attacked_With_Haki.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marco and Vista attack Akainu</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Akainu turned to launch another attack on Jinbe, and much to his annoyance was repelled by a simultaneous assault from Marco and Vista, who used <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Haki</a> to drive the admiral away from the injured Jinbe, Ace, and Luffy. Marco, deep in regret, wondered how they could have allowed all this to happen. As Ace spoke his last words to Luffy, Marco joined the battle in order to keep the Marine forces away from Ace<sup id="cite_ref-c574_31-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c574-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> and was seen crying after Ace had fallen dead.
</p><p>Determined to finish off Luffy, who was incapacitated from shock caused by his grief and anguish, Akainu attacked once again; this time he was again intercepted by Marco alone, who shouted that Akainu would not touch Luffy. He ordered Jinbe to take Luffy and go. As Luffy was all that remained of Ace's will, Marco declared that they would protect him without fail, in place of Ace; if he too were to die, the Whitebeard Pirates would be put to shame.<sup id="cite_ref-c575_32-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c575-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Whitebeard and Blackbeard confronted one another, Marco tried to fly to the other side of the giant crevice separating them to assist his captain, but was commanded to stay back by his captain, who said that he would kill Blackbeard as revenge for killing Thatch. When, consequently, Whitebeard was brutally killed by the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a> ganging up on him, Marco mourned Whitebeard's death as Whitebeard left the crew under his care.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Marco then witnessed Blackbeard revealing himself to have stolen, somehow, the power of the <a href="/wiki/Gura_Gura_no_Mi" title="Gura Gura no Mi">Gura Gura no Mi</a> from the dead Whitebeard, much to the commander's shock. Marco explained to a fellow crewmate that Blackbeard was no ordinary person, reasoning that Blackbeard's atypical body may have allowed him the aforementioned feat.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> Marco then joined his fellow crewmates, with some unlikely help from Crocodile, as they prepared to face off against Akainu to defend Luffy and carry him on to the next era.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> When <a href="/wiki/Koby" title="Koby">Koby</a> yelled for all the combatants to stop, Marco wondered why a Marine was trying to stop the fight.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Right after <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a> arrived at Marineford to stop the war, Marco was told by Shanks to withdraw peacefully from Marineford and avoid prolonging the battle any longer. Marco complied and later grieved with his crewmates over their losses.<sup id="cite_ref-c580_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c580-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-War_Arc">Post-War Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/51/Tomb_of_Ace_and_Whitebeard.png/revision/latest?cb=20230213180341" class="image"><img alt="Tomb of Ace and Whitebeard" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="225" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tomb of Ace and Whitebeard.png" data-image-key="Tomb_of_Ace_and_Whitebeard.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/51/Tomb_of_Ace_and_Whitebeard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230213180341" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/51/Tomb_of_Ace_and_Whitebeard.png/revision/latest?cb=20230213180341" class="image"><img alt="Tomb of Ace and Whitebeard" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/51/Tomb_of_Ace_and_Whitebeard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230213180341" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="225" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tomb of Ace and Whitebeard.png" data-image-key="Tomb_of_Ace_and_Whitebeard.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/51/Tomb_of_Ace_and_Whitebeard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230213180341" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tomb_of_Ace_and_Whitebeard.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marco and Shanks at Ace and Whitebeard's funeral.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Marсo, along with the rest of the crew, attended Ace and Whitebeard's funeral near Whitebeard's home of <a href="/wiki/Sphinx_(Location)" title="Sphinx (Location)">Sphinx</a> in the New World. He thanked Shanks for ensuring that Whitebeard and Ace received proper burials.<sup id="cite_ref-c590_24-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c590-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="During_the_Timeskip">During the Timeskip</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/23/Payback_War_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20231007042027" class="image"><img alt="Payback War Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="119" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Payback War Infobox.png" data-image-key="Payback_War_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/23/Payback_War_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231007042027" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/23/Payback_War_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20231007042027" class="image"><img alt="Payback War Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/23/Payback_War_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231007042027" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="119" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Payback War Infobox.png" data-image-key="Payback_War_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/23/Payback_War_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231007042027" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Payback_War_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marco vs. Blackbeard.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>One year after the war at Marineford, the remnants of the Whitebeard Pirates, under Marco's guidance, fought against the Blackbeard Pirates in the "<a href="/wiki/Payback_War" title="Payback War">Payback War</a>" in order to route an invading force, but suffered an overwhelming defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-c909_23-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c909-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Publicly, they are believed to have initiated the war to avenge their fallen comrades. They went into hiding and have not been seen since, which was what led Blackbeard to be officially recognized as Whitebeard's replacement among the Four Emperors.<sup id="cite_ref-c820_13-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c820-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Saga">Wano Country Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Arc">Wano Country Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After the Payback War, Marco went to Whitebeard's home village on <a href="/wiki/Sphinx_(Location)" title="Sphinx (Location)">Sphinx</a> and started working there as a doctor. Eventually, <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a> came there to find and try to recruit Marco into the <a href="/wiki/Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai_Alliance" title="Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance">alliance</a> formed to take down <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a> in <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>. In conversation with the <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">mink</a>, Marco mentioned <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a>'s history with said village, as well as how he had heard about <a href="/wiki/Edward_Weevil" title="Edward Weevil">Edward Weevil</a> attacking those connected to Whitebeard in search of a "fortune" that Marco noted did not exist. Because of the possibility that, in coming after him, Weevil would attack Sphinx as well, Marco voiced his decision to remain there to protect the village. Nonetheless, he asked Nekomamushi to pass on a message to <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a>:<sup id="cite_ref-c909_23-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c909-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> that he would still come to Wano, only late.<sup id="cite_ref-c982_69-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c982-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/12/Hoo-in.png/revision/latest?cb=20230113121545" class="image"><img alt="Hoo-in" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hoo-in.png" data-image-key="Hoo-in.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/12/Hoo-in.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230113121545" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/12/Hoo-in.png/revision/latest?cb=20230113121545" class="image"><img alt="Hoo-in" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/12/Hoo-in.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230113121545" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hoo-in.png" data-image-key="Hoo-in.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/12/Hoo-in.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230113121545" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hoo-in.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marco prevents the Big Mom Pirates from getting on Wano.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Days later in a surprising turn of events, Marco, who had decided to participate in the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Onigashima" title="Raid on Onigashima">Raid on Onigashima</a> after all, made his way to Wano at the same time as Nekomamushi and <a href="/wiki/Izou" title="Izou">Izou</a> (the latter of whom Marco knew the whereabouts of, hence them having made a pitstop to collect the <a href="/wiki/Samurai" title="Samurai">samurai</a>); this made Marco's message to Luffy unnecessary.<sup id="cite_ref-c982_69-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c982-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c984_70-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c984-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> During the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a>' second attempt at entering the country, Marco flew to their <a href="/wiki/Queen_Mama_Chanter" title="Queen Mama Chanter">ship</a> and, as it finished climbing the waterfall, knocked it back down using <a href="/wiki/Tori_Tori_no_Mi,_Model:_Phoenix#Techniques" title="Tori Tori no Mi, Model: Phoenix"><i>Hoo-in</i></a>.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> After Nekomamushi's ship had succeeded in going up the waterfall, Marco and the <a href="/wiki/Guardians" title="Guardians">Guardians</a> proceeded to <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c982_69-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c982-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> Once they reached the rear side of the island, a flying Marco dropped off Nekomamushi and Izou, and they encountered some of the <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</a> (including Izou's sister <a href="/wiki/Kikunojo" title="Kikunojo">Kikunojo</a>) alongside <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar Law</a>. As they rejoiced in their reunion, Marco said he would investigate a "strange shadow" he had spotted at sea earlier.<sup id="cite_ref-c984_70-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c984-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/80/Marco_vs._Big_Mom.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617141604" class="image"><img alt="Marco vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Marco vs. Big Mom.png" data-image-key="Marco_vs._Big_Mom.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/80/Marco_vs._Big_Mom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617141604" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/80/Marco_vs._Big_Mom.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617141604" class="image"><img alt="Marco vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/80/Marco_vs._Big_Mom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617141604" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Marco vs. Big Mom.png" data-image-key="Marco_vs._Big_Mom.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/80/Marco_vs._Big_Mom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617141604" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Marco_vs._Big_Mom.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marco clashes with Big Mom.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>He subsequently happened across <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> who proposed that they work together given their mutual goal of bringing down Kaidou,<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> and together they arrived at Onigashima's entrance.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> Eventually, the two encountered <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>, and Perospero bent to her will of upholding her alliance with Kaidou, with Marco noting that this spelt the end of their cooperation. When Big Mom asked why someone of Marco's status was helping some "<a href="/wiki/Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai_Alliance" title="Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance">brats</a>", saying that the remnants of the Whitebeard Pirates had lost their way, Marco simply asserted that, with Whitebeard's death, they were no longer bound to his will but left free to do as they pleased.<sup id="cite_ref-c992p4_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c992p4-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Marco then clashed against Big Mom, his phoenix flames proving capable of overpowering those of <a href="/wiki/Prometheus" title="Prometheus">Prometheus</a>. Big Mom grabbed Marco by the neck and ordered Perospero to kill him. However, before Perospero could fire his <a href="/wiki/Pero_Pero_no_Mi" title="Pero Pero no Mi">candy</a> bow and arrow at him, he was attacked by the <a href="/wiki/Sulong" title="Sulong">Sulong</a>-transformed <a href="/wiki/Wanda" title="Wanda">Wanda</a> and <a href="/wiki/Carrot" title="Carrot">Carrot</a>, who recognized Marco as Nekomamushi's ally. Big Mom abruptly decided to call off her fight with Marco and headed back to Kaidou's castle, with Wanda telling Marco to go after her. Marco then noticed a nearby commotion.<sup id="cite_ref-c995_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c995-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/54/Marco_Vs._All_Stars.png/revision/latest?cb=20220417055557" class="image"><img alt="Marco Vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Marco Vs. All Stars.png" data-image-key="Marco_Vs._All_Stars.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/54/Marco_Vs._All_Stars.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220417055557" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/54/Marco_Vs._All_Stars.png/revision/latest?cb=20220417055557" class="image"><img alt="Marco Vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/54/Marco_Vs._All_Stars.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220417055557" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Marco Vs. All Stars.png" data-image-key="Marco_Vs._All_Stars.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/54/Marco_Vs._All_Stars.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220417055557" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Marco_Vs._All_Stars.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marco facing King and Queen.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Afterwards, Marco reached the Live Floor within the <a href="/wiki/Skull_Dome" title="Skull Dome">Skull Dome</a> and offered to lend his assistance to the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hats</a> there.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> Proceeding to envelop the <a href="/wiki/Ice_Oni" title="Ice Oni">Ice Oni</a>-infected <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Chopper</a> with his flames to defrost him, Marco then started flying over and spreading his flames to all the infected present in the banquet hall, in order to slow the virus' freezing effects in those afflicted by raising their body heat. Once he had done so, Marco offered <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Zoro</a> and the other Straw Hats present to fly them to the Skull Dome's roof.<sup id="cite_ref-c998_45-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c998-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> As the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a> attacked Marco, he told <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Robin</a> to run into the castle. He then transformed into a phoenix and began carrying Zoro toward the roof. However, the All-Stars <a href="/wiki/King" title="King">King</a> and <a href="/wiki/Queen" title="Queen">Queen</a> made an attempt to stop their advancement upward, with Queen shooting at Marco.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> Despite the All-Stars' efforts, however, Marco managed to hold them back with his phoenix wings and successfully threw Zoro up to the roof through the hole in it.<sup id="cite_ref-c1000_34-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1000-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4c/King_Vs_Marco.png/revision/latest?cb=20220623075043" class="image"><img alt="King Vs Marco" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="King Vs Marco.png" data-image-key="King_Vs_Marco.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4c/King_Vs_Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220623075043" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4c/King_Vs_Marco.png/revision/latest?cb=20220623075043" class="image"><img alt="King Vs Marco" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4c/King_Vs_Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220623075043" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="King Vs Marco.png" data-image-key="King_Vs_Marco.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4c/King_Vs_Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220623075043" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:King_Vs_Marco.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marco fighting King.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Marco then began fighting King and, while being assaulted by him, heard <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>'s cry for help broadcasted throughout Onigashima, which he was amused by.<sup id="cite_ref-c1005_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1005-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Sometime after, Marco intercepted Queen's attempt at hitting <a href="/wiki/Hyougoro" title="Hyougoro">Hyougoro</a> with a <a href="/wiki/Ryu_Ryu_no_Mi,_Model:_Brachiosaurus#Techniques" title="Ryu Ryu no Mi, Model: Brachiosaurus">laser shot from his mouth</a>, striking and injuring the All-Star with <i>Hoo-in</i>. Marco reminded Queen that, since they were fighting, Queen ought to not even think of about the samurai until he had finished Marco off. Marco then flew toward Queen, dodging another laser, as King suddenly jumped in and cut off Marco's left phoenix wing. Marco, unfazed, simply reshaped the wing's feathery remains into a large fireball that, as his <i>Bluebird</i> attack, he sent toward King, sending him violently crashing into a nearby building. Before King could properly guard himself, Marco followed up with a flying knee strike, causing an explosion where King had landed. As Queen angrily approached, he was suddenly hit by yet another attack from Marco, <i>Ongle</i>: a taloned kick that sent him flying as well. Marco noted how holding off two men with <a href="/wiki/Bounties" title="Bounties">bounties</a> over a billion was difficult, telling Chopper to hurry up.<sup id="cite_ref-c1006_36-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1006-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Chopper had successfully created a <a href="/wiki/Chopperphage" title="Chopperphage">counter-virus</a> neutralizing Queen's Ice Oni, and an enraged Queen was distracted by his subordinates turning on him for his treating them expendable, Marco took the chance to grab hold of Queen's neck, restraining him to allow Chopper to slap Queen in his <a href="/wiki/Hito_Hito_no_Mi#Monster_Point" title="Hito Hito no Mi">Monster Point</a> form. As Chopper exclaimed that he was not a "tanuki", Marco inwardly apologized for having called him such,<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> before he and Chopper continued engaging Queen.<sup id="cite_ref-ep1025_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ep1025-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> A little thereafter, Marco reacted with concern about the broadcasted announcement that Luffy, the highest bounty head on the alliance's side, had been defeated by Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> When Sanji arrived in time to save Chopper from Queen, declaring how not all hope was lost, Marco commented how this was why he liked their crew.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A while later, Marco was seen sitting still on the ground, having seemingly reached the limit of his stamina. This gave King and Queen the opportunity to wipe out significant portions of the enemy alliance without distraction, including the turncoat Beasts Pirates. When King confronted a bandaged-up Zoro, who was being carried away by samurai, the All-Star tried attacking him with a <a href="/wiki/King#Attacks" title="King">flaming punch</a>, but just then Marco flew in to block it with his <i>Fujiazami</i> technique. Marco remarked that he had long ago heard about a <a href="/wiki/Lunarians" title="Lunarians">certain race</a> living atop the <a href="/wiki/Red_Line" title="Red Line">Red Line</a> that could burst into flames, which King left uncommented. As King and Queen then prepared to attack Marco and take him out for good, Marco stated with a smile that he had done his part and would now allow the star players to take the stage; right then, a recovered Zoro and Sanji jumped in, launching an attack on King and Queen respectively.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Zoro and Sanji's attack, Marco watched King and Queen rise back up. Intrigued, he remembered something once told him by Whitebeard: about how long before <a href="/wiki/Mary_Geoise" title="Mary Geoise">Mary Geoise</a> existed, there had been a land of gods on top of the Red Line. While absorbed in these thoughts, some Beasts Pirates shot at him. Izou arrived in time, grabbed hold of Marco to dodge the gunfire, and then ran away with Marco under his arm. Marco jokingly noted how had waited to be saved by him, then asked Izou if he believed in gods, prompting Izou to say that Marco was sounding just like a drunk Whitebeard.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> A while later, Marco and Izou were still on the Live Stage, reacting shocked at the sight of Queen separating his brachiosaurus neck and tail from the rest of his body to attack Sanji.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Afterwards, Marco in his full phoenix form began carrying Izou over the Live Stage and towards Kaidou's burning castle, where they had heard was some kind of large <a href="/wiki/Kazenbo" title="Kazenbo">fire apparition</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> Sometime later, Marco was seen again in the bath of the Skull Dome's Forehead Floor, having met up with <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> and having just finished healing the two beasts <a href="/wiki/Komachiyo" title="Komachiyo">Komachiyo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hihimaru" title="Hihimaru">Hihimaru</a> for <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Tama" title="Kurozumi Tama">Tama</a>. Marco remarked that it was important for them to keep their wits about them with how fast things were developing, stating that as of that moment, Onigashima was the most dangerous island in the world.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> It was soon thereafter that Kaidou came back down from the Skull Dome's rooftop, declaring his victory over Luffy. When the Emperor attempted to hit Nami with his <i><a href="/wiki/Uo_Uo_no_Mi,_Model:_Seiryu#Kaidou" title="Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu">Bolo Breath</a></i>, Marco jumped in using <i>Fujiazami</i> to shield her from the attack, at the same time declaring to his comrades that they ought not to lose their composure so long as not everything was over.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sure enough, Marco was afterwards among the few people on the Live Floor that <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">sensed</a> how Luffy was still conscious, telling Nami and Tama as much.<sup id="cite_ref-c1044_47-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1044-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Luffy then resumed his battle with Kaidou, during which Marco witnessed Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_5_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 5 Techniques">giant head</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> Not long after, the Straw Hat successfully defeated Kaidou, an event that coincided with the island of Onigashima finally landing after Kaidou had made it float all the way next to the Flower Capital. Marco was seen standing near Nami and Tama, watching them celebrate their alliance's victory against the Beasts Pirates with a smile on his face.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/Marco_and_Samurai_Paying_Respects_to_the_Fallen.png/revision/latest?cb=20231102121051" class="image"><img alt="Marco and Samurai Paying Respects to the Fallen" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Marco and Samurai Paying Respects to the Fallen.png" data-image-key="Marco_and_Samurai_Paying_Respects_to_the_Fallen.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/Marco_and_Samurai_Paying_Respects_to_the_Fallen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231102121051" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/Marco_and_Samurai_Paying_Respects_to_the_Fallen.png/revision/latest?cb=20231102121051" class="image"><img alt="Marco and Samurai Paying Respects to the Fallen" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/Marco_and_Samurai_Paying_Respects_to_the_Fallen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231102121051" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Marco and Samurai Paying Respects to the Fallen.png" data-image-key="Marco_and_Samurai_Paying_Respects_to_the_Fallen.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/Marco_and_Samurai_Paying_Respects_to_the_Fallen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231102121051" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Marco_and_Samurai_Paying_Respects_to_the_Fallen.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marco and the Samurai paying respects to the fallen.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>A week following the raid on Onigashima, Marco was seen at the <a href="/wiki/Ringo#Northern_Cemetery" title="Ringo">Northern Cemetery of Ringo</a> with <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin&#39;emon">Kin'emon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kawamatsu" title="Kawamatsu">Kawamatsu</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Onimaru" title="Onimaru">Onimaru</a>. When Kin'emon asked Marco if he was fine with Izou, who had lost his life in the raid, being buried in Ringo, Marco responded that it was only right for Izou to have his home country become his final resting place. Marco solemnly commented that he was once again left with one of his comrades dead, with Kin'emon and Kawamatsu noting that they knew the feeling.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> Before he departed Wano, he visited Luffy, Jinbe, Zoro and Sanji who were in a discussion with Yamato, and bid them farewell since he was leaving with the <a href="/wiki/Red_Hair_Pirates" title="Red Hair Pirates">Red Hair Pirates</a>. After receiving thanks from Luffy, Marco told them that they would now carry the new age on their shoulder.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="One_Piece_Film:_Red">One Piece Film: Red</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Marco and the villagers listened to <a href="/wiki/Uta" title="Uta">Uta</a>'s childhood song "<a href="/wiki/Where_the_Wind_Blows" title="Where the Wind Blows">Where the Wind Blows</a>" from the <a href="/wiki/Dials#Tone_Dial" title="Dials">Tone Dial</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>
<small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_Saga">Final Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D43&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Egghead_Arc">Egghead Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D44&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As the Red Force neared Sphinx, Marco thanked the Red Hair Pirates for picking him up, though he cheerfully shut down Shanks' attempts at recruiting him, saying he was done babysitting bigger pirate groups, and felt he was getting too old for such affairs. So, Marco effectively retired from a life of piracy, and then flew off towards Sphinx.<sup id="cite_ref-c1059_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1059-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bd/Miss_Buckin_encounters_Marco.png/revision/latest?cb=20240729220129" class="image"><img alt="Miss Buckin encounters Marco" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="136" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Miss Buckin encounters Marco.png" data-image-key="Miss_Buckin_encounters_Marco.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bd/Miss_Buckin_encounters_Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240729220129" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bd/Miss_Buckin_encounters_Marco.png/revision/latest?cb=20240729220129" class="image"><img alt="Miss Buckin encounters Marco" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bd/Miss_Buckin_encounters_Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240729220129" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="136" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Miss Buckin encounters Marco.png" data-image-key="Miss_Buckin_encounters_Marco.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bd/Miss_Buckin_encounters_Marco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240729220129" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Miss_Buckin_encounters_Marco.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Miss Buckin informs Marco of Weavil's predicament.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When he reached the Island, he encountered the villagers that told him that the Marines invaded during his absence, but they were driven away by <a href="/wiki/Edward_Weevil" title="Edward Weevil">Edward Weevil</a>. Just then a frantic <a href="/wiki/Buckingham_Stussy" title="Buckingham Stussy">Miss Buckin</a> revealed that Weevil was defeated and arrested by Admiral <a href="/wiki/Aramaki" title="Aramaki">Ryokugyu</a>. While he was grateful for Weevil's help, Buckin could tell from Marco's tone he was still doubtful that the former warlord was Whitebeard's biological son so she told him she knew someone who could prove it; <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Dr. Vegapunk</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> Later as he listened to <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a>'s worldwide broadcast, Marco recalled what Whitebeard said about the Lunarians and the Red Line when the scientist mentioned rare <a href="/wiki/Race" title="Race">races</a> that were persecuted.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Major_Battles">Major Battles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D45&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<ul><li>Marco vs. <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a></li>

<li>Marco vs. <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Monkey D. Garp</a></li>

Ace">Ace</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thatch" title="Thatch">Thatch</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jozu" title="Jozu">Jozu</a>), <a href="/wiki/Crocodile" title="Crocodile">Crocodile</a> and <a href="/wiki/Andre" title="Andre">Andre</a> vs. Akainu</li></ul></li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Manga_and_Anime_Differences">Manga and Anime Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D46&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In the anime when Marco was first shown, his design was replaced with a more generic one of a dark-haired crewmember<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> (whereas the manga correctly showed him having light-colored hair). This is a common mistake that occurs in transferring a scene from manga to anime and has been witnessed in <i>One Piece</i> before, in particular when characters are first shown <a href="/wiki/Silvers_Rayleigh#Anime_and_Manga_Differences" title="Silvers Rayleigh">without a formal introduction</a>.
</p><p>In the anime, in the flashback showing the final battle between the Whitebeard and <a href="/wiki/Roger_Pirates" title="Roger Pirates">Roger Pirates</a>, a teenaged Marco was shown clashing with <a href="/wiki/Silvers_Rayleigh" title="Silvers Rayleigh">Silvers Rayleigh</a>, the latter able to stop Marco's phoenix kick using a single <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki#Emission" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Haki</a>-imbued finger.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D47&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 100px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/28/Portrait_of_Pirates_Marco_Figurine.png/revision/latest?cb=20150308232147" class="image"><img alt="Portrait of Pirates Marco Figurine" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="100" height="212" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Portrait of Pirates Marco Figurine.png" data-image-key="Portrait_of_Pirates_Marco_Figurine.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/28/Portrait_of_Pirates_Marco_Figurine.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20150308232147" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/28/Portrait_of_Pirates_Marco_Figurine.png/revision/latest?cb=20150308232147" class="image"><img alt="Portrait of Pirates Marco Figurine" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/28/Portrait_of_Pirates_Marco_Figurine.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20150308232147" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="100" height="212" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Portrait of Pirates Marco Figurine.png" data-image-key="Portrait_of_Pirates_Marco_Figurine.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/28/Portrait_of_Pirates_Marco_Figurine.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20150308232147" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Portrait_of_Pirates_Marco_Figurine.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Portrait of Pirates figurine of Marco.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Marco has been featured in various figurine series, such as <a href="/wiki/Portrait_of_Pirates" title="Portrait of Pirates">Portrait of Pirates</a> or <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_World_Collectable_Figure" title="One Piece World Collectable Figure">One Piece World Collectable Figure</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Video_Games_2">Video Games</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D48&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
