<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Appearances">Other Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D51&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Media">Other Media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D52&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>In <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Premier_Show#One_Piece_Premier_Show_2012" title="One Piece Premier Show">One Piece Premier Show 2012</a>, Marco travels to <a href="/wiki/Samba_Island" title="Samba Island">Samba Island</a> to pursue the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a> pirate <a href="/wiki/Chameleone" title="Chameleone">Chameleone</a>, who had disaffiliated from the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a> after killing some of his allies. Marco and Luffy work together to defeat him. Marco also appears in <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Premier_Show_2017" title="One Piece Premier Show 2017">One Piece Premier Show 2017</a> during the retelling of the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>.</li>
<li>"MEMORIAL WALL ~Remember Marineford~", one of the Photo Spots in <a href="/wiki/Tokyo_One_Piece_Tower" title="Tokyo One Piece Tower">Tokyo One Piece Tower</a>, features a statue of Marco next to an image projection wall.</li>
<li>Marco appears in <a href="/wiki/Super_Kabuki_II:_One_Piece" title="Super Kabuki II: One Piece">Super Kabuki II: One Piece</a> during the retelling of the <a href="/wiki/Marineford_Arc" title="Marineford Arc">Marineford Arc</a>.</li>
<li>Marco appears in Marineford version of the <a href="/wiki/Hungry_Days" title="Hungry Days">Hungry Days</a> commercial.</li></ul>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 172px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 172px; height: 172px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bb/Marco_Premiere_Show.png/revision/latest?cb=20130128003243" class="image"><img alt="Marco Premiere Show" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="89" height="150" data-image-name="Marco Premiere Show.png" data-image-key="Marco_Premiere_Show.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bb/Marco_Premiere_Show.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/89?cb=20130128003243" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Marco as he appears in the One Piece Premier Show 2012.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 172px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 172px; height: 172px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b1/Memorial_Wall_Marco_Statue.png/revision/latest?cb=20201117025448" class="image"><img alt="Memorial Wall Marco Statue" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="113" data-image-name="Memorial Wall Marco Statue.png" data-image-key="Memorial_Wall_Marco_Statue.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b1/Memorial_Wall_Marco_Statue.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20201117025448" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">A statue of Marco in "MEMORIAL WALL ~Remember Marineford~".
</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D53&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>In the 4th, 5th, 6th, and 7th <a href="/wiki/Popularity_Polls" title="Popularity Polls">fan polls</a> of most popular characters, Marco was ranked 122nd, 12th, 20th, and 19th, respectively. Being in the last two, he was the second most popular member of the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a> behind <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Ace</a>.</li>
<li>Marco's pineapple-like haircut and gag of being compared to a pineapple<sup id="cite_ref-c820_13-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c820-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> likely reference an older Japanese term for pineapples, <i>hōri</i><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">鳳梨</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, which can translate to "phoenix pear" (referring to the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fenghuang" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Fenghuang">Chinese fenghuang</a>), as a nod to his abilities. One of Marco's attacks also contains that very word for pineapple.<sup id="cite_ref-c998_45-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c998-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Marco is the first person revealed to have eaten a <a href="/wiki/Zoan#Mythical_Zoan" title="Zoan">Mythical Zoan</a>-type Devil Fruit, when its concept is first introduced.</li>
<li>Marco's favorite food is pineapple as a play on his in-story comparison to the fruit, and his least favorite food is beans.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Marco's animal resemblance is a phoenix, a reference to his Devil Fruit's abilities.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Marco's hobby is collecting bar coasters.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="SBS-Based_Trivia">SBS-Based Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FMarco%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D54&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Marco's birthday, October 5th, comes from his name as a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_wordplay#Numeric_substitution" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Japanese wordplay">goroawase</a>-type pun: 10/5 gives 0/5, with a <i>kun'yomi</i> reading of "zero" being "maru" and an <i>on'yomi</i> reading of "five" being "ko" in Japanese, hence playing on Marco's name as pronounced in Japanese: "Maruko"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">マルコ</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-Birth_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Birth-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>A fan asked <a href="/wiki/Eiichiro_Oda" title="Eiichiro Oda">Oda</a> if Marco's penis would regenerate if it was cut off, and Oda answered that it would.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
